u = urllib.request.urlopen(url)
f = open(file_name, 'wb')
meta = u.info()
file_size = int(meta.getheaders('Content-Length')[0])
print(('Downloading: %s Bytes: %s' % (file_name, file_size)))
file_size_dl = 0
block_sz = 8192
while True:
    buffer = u.read(block_sz)
    if (not buffer):
        break
    file_size_dl += len(buffer)
    f.write(buffer)
    status = ('%10d  [%3.2f%%]' % (file_size_dl, ((file_size_dl * 100.0) / file_size)))
    status = (status + (chr(8) * (len(status) + 1)))
    print(status, end=' ')
f.close()	download a file over HTTP	download a file `url` over HTTP and save to `file_name`
response = urllib.request.urlopen('http://www.example.com/')
html = response.read()	download a file over HTTP	download a file 'http://www.example.com/' over HTTP

u = urllib.request.urlopen(url)
f = open(file_name, 'wb')
meta = u.info()
file_size = int(meta.getheaders('Content-Length')[0])
print(('Downloading: %s Bytes: %s' % (file_name, file_size)))
file_size_dl = 0
block_sz = 8192
while True:
    buffer = u.read(block_sz)
    if (not buffer):
        break
    file_size_dl += len(buffer)
    f.write(buffer)
    status = ('%10d  [%3.2f%%]' % (file_size_dl, ((file_size_dl * 100.0) / file_size)))
    status = (status + (chr(8) * (len(status) + 1)))
    print(status, end=' ')
f.close()	download a file over HTTP	download a file `url` over HTTP and save to `file_name`
response = urllib.request.urlopen('http://www.example.com/')
html = response.read()	download a file over HTTP	download a file 'http://www.example.com/' over HTTP

def bufcount(filename):
    f = open(filename)
    lines = 0
    buf_size = (1024 * 1024)
    read_f = f.read
    buf = read_f(buf_size)
    while buf:
        lines += buf.count('\n')
        buf = read_f(buf_size)
    return lines	get line count	get line count of file `filename`
